# <a name="obsolete-members-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-102">Membres obsolètes dans le .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-102">Obsolete Members in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-103">Les tableaux de cet article répertorient les membres de type obsolètes dans le [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] \(y compris ses versions intermédiaires, telles que le [!INCLUDE[net_v451](../../../includes/net-v451-md.md)]\) et le [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] \(y compris ses versions intermédiaires\), organisés par assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-103">The tables in this article list the type members that are obsolete in the              [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] \(including its point releases, such as              [!INCLUDE[net_v451](../../../includes/net-v451-md.md)]\) and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] \(including its point releases\), organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-104">Utilisez les liens suivants pour consulter la liste des membres obsolètes et des alternatives recommandées dans chaque assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete members and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-105">Cette rubrique ne répertorie pas les membres des types obsolètes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-105">This topic doesn't list the members of obsolete types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-106">Pour obtenir la liste des types obsolètes, consultez [Types obsolètes](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-106">For a list of obsolete types, see              [Obsolete Types](../../../docs/framework/whats-new/obsolete-types.md).</span></span>

## <a name="obsolete-members-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-140">Membres obsolètes dans les assemblys système</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-140">Obsolete Members in System Assemblies</span></span>  
 <span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-141">Les tableaux suivants répertorient les membres obsolètes dans les assemblys système.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-141">The following tables list the obsolete members in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ba1b2-142">Ces assemblys sont utilisés pour le développement d’applications à usage général qui ciblent le .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ba1b2-142">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
